</font><font color="#00FFFF">A Small Glade
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">   The dense canopy found elsewhere in the haunted forest thins out, giving way
to a small glade.  Flowers and fauna flourish here, unhindered in their growth
by the trees which otherwise choke new growth in the ancient woods.  A narrow
path weaves peacefully through the glade, leading towards the north, east, and
west.
